【ai】〔ʔa³³〕〔ʕa³³〕
◇动, vt
●欠 to owe:
☆Ngaf zzee ddeegvl nee gai cheenihal jelye ddeemaiq tv bel hee nal, eyi teiq dal ai melsei. @ 我的朋友前几天向我借了一点钱，但是现在还欠着呢。 A friend borrowed some money a few days ago, and (lit: but now) (he) still owes (it to me).
☆Ngeq gai cheenihal jelye zeiq jigaiq yil, xi gol ddeemaiq tv nal, cheekaq la teiq dal ai melsei. @ 前一段时间我急需用钱，就跟别人借了点儿，可是到现在还欠着呢。 I've had a lot of expenses lately, so (I) borrowed some money. And (lit: but now) (I) still owe (it).
■参见{rhu#2}
✧ rhu ai 
◇短语, phr
●欠债 to owe a debt (of sth)
◇助动, auxv
●该(做)，应(得)，理所当然 to deserve to (because it is owed to you), to need to (because of a sense of duty):
☆Lobbeixi nee gapv ddee chee ddee ai meq. @ 做工的人得工钱是应该的。 Laborers deserve to receive (their) wages.
☆Ssomil nee ebbamei vqree chee ai meq. @ 儿女赡养父母是应该的。 Children need to serve/honor their parents.

【ba】〔pɑ³³〕
◇动, vt
●到(某地或某时) to arrive, to reach (a destination or a time), to get to:
☆Cheekaq gol ba me ceeq chee, tee ezee bbei neiq keel me ddoq wei. @ 到现在都不来，真不知他在干什么？(He) still hasn't arrived even now. What can he be doing?
☆Ngeq soqni sher ddeemerq jju yil, chuq bbei rhee loq ba ner. @ 明天我有点事，必须很早到城里去。 I have a little matter to deal with tomorrow, so (I) must get to town early.
■同义词{da}, {tv#1}
◇助动, auxv
●好(表示达到完美的程度) to complete (used as a complement of an action to indicate the desired outcome):
☆Bbiuq cheedduq niaiq ba pil seil, bbv teiq ku yi. @ 揉好这团面以后，再把锅预热。 After the dough has been kneaded, heat the wok.

【ba】〔pɑ³³〕

☆Kaqzzei dvq mai ddeenihal ggv seiq yil, ba hol neiq seiq. @ 玉米种下去有一段时间了，快出苗了。 It has already been several days since (we) planted corn, so (it) will sprout very soon.
☆Ssiulssiuq cheegvl walhei ggv seiq yil, hee ni'liu teiq ba seiq. @ 这孩子五个月大了，已长了两颗牙。 This child is five months old, and (he) already has two teeth.

【bbaq】〔bɑ²¹〕
◇动, vt
●开(花) (flowers) to bloom:
☆Cheekaq bbalbba bbaq neiq. @ 现在花正在开放。 The flowers are blooming now.
◇量, cls
●朵 for flowers or blossoms:
☆Bbalbba ddeenibbaq peel tal. @ 可以摘几朵花。(You) can pick several flowers.
◇尾, suf
●花 flower:
☆Cheenihal leilbbaq bbaq rheeq me waq see. @ 现在还不是开茶花的时候。 These days, it still isn't time for the camellia flowers to bloom.
■同义词{bbalbba}
◇动, vt
●出(天花) (for smallpox pustules) to appear:
☆Gainief seil, aiqpi bbaq chee jjaiq malma jjeq gge ddeegguq waq yil, xi sseidde ddeebeil chee aiqpi bbaq gol nee shee seiq. @ 以前天花是一种很难治的病，很多人都因为出天花而死了。 In the past, smallpox was a difficult disease to cure. Therefore, many people died from smallpox.
✧ aiqpi bbaq 
◇短语, phr
出天花 for smallpox pustules to appear, to have smallpox

☆Ssuilssuif qil zherq me niq, bba'laq ddeemerq bbeeq bbei muq zherq naiq. @ 别让孩子着凉，给他们多穿点衣服。 Don't let the kids get cold. Put a little more clothing on (them).

【bbei】〔be³³〕

●做，干 to do (general term):
☆Tee jjaiq jigaiq bbei lo bbei neiq ye. @ 他正忙着干活。 He is busily doing (his) work.
☆Tei'ee bbei sei pil seil, ggaihee bbee tal seiq. @ 做完作业后，就可以去玩了。 After (you) finish (your) homework, then (you) can go play.
☆Ezee bbei neiq lei? @ 你在干什么？ What are (you) doing?
✧ bbei me bbee 
◇短语, phr
●懒 lazy
✧ bbeizo 
◇名, n
●事情 sth to do:
☆Ngeq cheeni taf goq baba keel mei, jjaif siuq bbeizo me jju meq yil, lei wul ceeq seiq. @ 我今天到他们家去帮忙，但没什么事可做，所以就回来了。 I went to their house to help today. But there was nothing to do, so (I) came home.
●作为，当 to be, to serve as, to act as:
☆Tee seeqzzee bbei ceiqkvl hal ggv seiq. @ 她当十多年的老师了。 She has been a teacher for more than ten years.
✧ sui bbei

●安抚 to comfort, to encourage
✧ nvlmei bbei

☆Ngeq cheeni ggvzzeiq pielpie yil, ngaf bba gai ddeemaiq rer mei, nge gge nvlmei lei bbei yel ceeq ye. @ 我今天弄坏了东西，有点怕我爸，但是他反而过来安慰我。 Today I broke something and was afraid (of what) my father (might say), but (he) actually comforted me.

【bbei】〔be³³〕
◇助, ptcl
●地(副词化词) adverbializer; particle which creates adverbial clauses (or phrases) of manner:
☆Cheeni daiche pil, ngeq seiq bbei bbei ner lei? @ 今天把单车弄丢了，我该怎么办呢？(My) bike was stolen today. What should I do?
☆Ddeemaiq chuq bbei jji! @ 走快一点。 Walk a little faster!
☆Sai'laiq gv bber'lerl dal waq bbei teiq jal ye. @ 桌子上尽是苍蝇。 The table is covered with flies which have landed (there).
☆Ceel qer talrheeq zzerq chee shuaq rua seiqmei, zzer'laq la me gogoq yil, nvlmei me zeiq bbei ggeq chual bbeef seil, meeq bai shee gvl. @ 黑枣树非常高，树枝也脆，爬上去要是不小心，会摔死的。 Date-plum persimmon trees are very tall, and the branches are not sturdy. If (you) do not carefully climb up, (you) can fall flat on the ground and die.
◇助, ptcl
●(把认知动词、语音动词、知觉动词等等的宾语作标记，特别是——但不一定——当宾语是嵌入句的时候) (marks the object of verbs of cognition, speech, perception and so on, especially, but not exclusively, when the object is an embedded clause):
☆Kvlpai ddeeq gge mil gol la elnai bbei shel. @ 上了年纪的女人也可以叫奶奶。 Any elderly woman is also called grandmother.
☆Teeggeeq nee sso cheegvl siul naiq'vf bbei seeddv neiq ye. @ 他们在想杀那个男人。 They are considering killing that man.
◇副, adv
●都 all, both (general term):
☆"Eq, hualleiq!" Ngeq leel shel me sei melsei nee, ngaf mo neif nge zzee nigvl bbei cheekaq nee shel mei, "Me waq, hualleiqddvq me." “ @ 哦，是人家的猫”。我还没说完，我妈妈和我的两个朋友都说：“不是嘛，是野猫。” I had not even finished saying, "Hey, a housecat!" when my mother and two friends all suddenly said, "No, (it's) a leopard cat."
☆Kual neif ersherq bbei jjiq cerqtv bbi nee siadvf naiq. @ 碗筷都要用开水消毒。 Bowls and chopsticks should all be sterilized in boiling water.

【bbei】〔be³³〕〔mbe³³〕
◇形, adj
●薄 thin (e.g. paper, ice or any flat object):
☆Ngaf ddiuq gge gusiashel loq nee qi neiq gge seellial bofmoq chee jjaiq bbei ye. @ 我们那儿的供销社所卖的塑料薄膜很薄。 The plastic sheeting that my community's co-op store sells is very thin.
☆Ngeq bba'laq muq bbei yel, qil nee ngaiq me loq ye. @ 我穿的衣服太薄了，冷得受不了。 The clothes I'm wearing are thin, so (I'm) so cold (I) can hardly take it.
■相关词{lal#3}
■同义词{bbei'leil}
●稀少，稀疏 sparse, thinly spaced (e.g. corn which didn't sprout well):
☆Kaqzzei cheepeil cheedde bbei chee bbeeddiq nee zzee mei waq. @ 这块玉米地如此稀疏是因为虫吃的缘故。 This field of corn is this sparse because the bugs ate (it) up.
☆Xi cheegvl gge gv'fv jjaif bbei ye; cheegvl ddeemerq el gguq keel ddaq? @ 这个人的头发太稀了，会不会是有病呢？ This guy's hair is very sparse. Has he perhaps been sick?
■相关词{lal#3}
●浅 shallow (e.g. water in a lake):
☆Eyihal heeq me ggee yil, Ci'leq hoq gge jjiq la jjaiq bbei ye. @ 这段时间因为没下雨，青龙河里水变得很浅。 Qinglong River is very shallow, because it hasn't rained recently.
☆Rer me ner, jjihoq bbei meq yil, jjiq gai caq bel lu laq. @ 不要怕，河很浅。蹚过来吧！ Don't worry, the river is shallow. Wade on across.
■相关词{hol#1}

【通常可以省略成一个升调加到前一个音节，整个句子的意思不变。 In a sentence, this word may be partially deleted, becoming a floating tone that attaches to the preceding syllable. If the preceding syllable has a mid or low tone, it will be articulated as a rising tone. The original meaning is retained:
☆Cheeni rhee loq nee ddeesiuq haiq bel ceeq. @ 今天从城里买来一样东西。(I) bought something in town today and brought it back. (Or:
☆Buying something in town, I came home.)
☆Cheeni rhee loq nee ddeesiuq haif ceeq. @ 今天从城里买来一样东西。(I) bought something in town today and brought it back. (Or:
☆Buying something in town, I came home.)
☆Seeqzzee cheegvl meheeq bel ceeq yil, tee nee ssossiul chee nigvl dol shel, "Naf nigvl jalsheef loq hiul me to." @ 老师生气了，她就对那两个男生说：“你们俩别呆在教室里了。” The teacher became angry, so she said to those two boys, "You two may not stay in the classroom."

◇数, num
●十四 fourteen •当后接的音节为底调或升调时，发中调“lu”；当后接的音节为高调时，发高调“lul”，同时后接的音节变为中调；其他情况发高调“lul”。 The second syllable "lu" is pronounced with a high tone when followed by a high or mid tone word, triggering the high tone of the following word to change to mid tone.

It is pronounced with a mid tone when followed by a word with a low or rising tone.

◇副, adv

☆Chee ddeesiuq dal waq meq. ( = Chee ddeesiuf waq meq.) @ 这都是一样的。 It is the same.

☆Nge nee kukee teiq hiul bbei ddee ler'lerq nee mei, tee meeqdiul jjeq ceeq ye. @ 我站在门口一喊，他就跑出来了。 Standing at (his) doorway, I called once, and he came running out.

◇短语, phr

☆Zzee me gvl la me ner, ddee so neiq tal. @ 不会吃没关系，可以尝一下。 If (you) don't like (it), never mind. Just taste (it) once.
●全，整，满 all, whole:
☆Nee gge ggaiheezo ggeq seelsee pil, ddeeddiuq bbei teiq gulgu me to. @ 把你的玩具收起来，不要丢得满地都是。 Pick up your toys. Don't throw them all around (i.e. one〔whole〕place).
☆Jigueq ddee'liu ni nvl, ddeeggoq ni lei? @ 要一整个南瓜，还是要一瓣？ Do (you) want one whole pumpkin or just a section?
☆Cheeni Aldeif bber tvl yil, Meeqddiuqwe ddeebbei bbei taf goq jjuq ye. @ 今天阿德结

【婚，整个中心村的人都到他家了。 Today Adei is hosting people (i.e. getting married), and the whole village (i.e. one】〔whole〕village) of Zhongxin is at his house.
☆Ello cheegvl yagoq xi neif ssomil me jjuq yil, ddeecherl bbei nge nee vqree, nge gol dal zherq bbee. @ 因为这个老爷爷无亲无故的，我想让他跟我一起住，让他能老有所终。 I am going to let this grandpa live with me so I can take care (of him) the rest of (his) life (i.e. one〔whole〕life), because he has no family or children.

elchee】〔ʔɑ⁵⁵ʈʂʰʅ³³〕
◇代, pron
●那(指示代词，多用于指代表某段时间，也可指代表某个地点。若是指代表人或物时，一般指的是相对不突出的那一方) that (marked demonstrative, indicating a contrast to the current referent; most commonly used with time words and place words):
☆Keeni cheemei ddaf ngaf gge waq ye nal, elcheemei eneif gge waq keel me see. @ 这只狗是我家的，但那一只就不知道是谁家的了。 This dog is ours, but (I) don't know whose dog that one is.
☆Ngeq gainieq Kuimiq walkv hiul jji. Elcheerheeq seil, Diaicheeq gge jjiq chee eyi nilniq bbei me dderq yil, ngeq neif ngaf zzee ddeenigvl sseidde bbei elchee'loq ggaihee ser. @ 我以前曾在昆明呆过五年。那时滇池的水没有现在浑，我和几个朋友很喜欢去那里玩。 I formerly lived in Kunming for five years. At that time, several friends and I liked to go to Dianchi Lake for fun, because it was not as dirty as it is now.

◇助动, auxv
●好(指可吃的、用的) to be safe (to eat or to use) •多用于否定式。 Most commonly used in the negative:
☆Zzee ga me ga me see gge mul seil, seel me niq. @ 不知道能不能吃的菌子，就不要采。 Don't pick mushrooms if (you) don't know whether (they) are safe to eat or not.

☆Shee cheekual zzee me ga sie. @ 这碗肉不能吃了。 This bowl of meat is not safe to eat.
◇动, vt
●待(某人)好 to treat (sb) well, to be good or kind (to sb):
☆Taf chermei cheegvl yuqpei yuqmei gol sseidde ga ye. @ 他家这个媳妇对公公婆婆真是好孝顺。 The daughter-in-law in their family is so good to (her) father-in-law and mother-in-law.
☆Tee nee nge gol cheesiuq ga chee, ngeq ddeecherl lei mil me tal seiq. @ 他待我这么好，我一辈子也忘不了。 He has been so kind towards me. How could I ever (i.e. in my whole life) forget (him)?

【ggeq】〔ɡɤ²¹〕
◇形, adj
●满意 satisfied:
☆Ngaf sso gge gguq leel lei ga seil, ngeq shee bbee la ggeq seiq. @ 只要我儿子的病好了，我死也无憾。 If my son recovers from (his) illness, I can die with no regrets (i.e. satisfied).
●甘心 be resigned to (sth) •一般用于否定句或疑问句。 This word is usually used in the negative:
☆Cheesseeq qeq lal loq tafggeeq ddee'liu nee xi gai pil pil yil, sseidde me ggeq neiq ye. @ 这次球赛他们以一球之差输了，很不甘心呢。

【They lost this basketball game by only one basket, and (they're) still not resigned to it.

ggv】〔ɡvv³³〕

☆Naf bbuqnal sseidde ddaq ggv lei? Ngaf

【gge bbuqnal seeqxijiq hal ddaq ggv ye. @ 你家的大肥猪有多少斤？我家的大肥猪有三百多斤。 How much does your hog weigh? Our hog weighs more than 300 pounds.
☆Naf gge erq jjaif sherq ddeekeeq jju zeel yel, ssei sherq ddaq ggv lei? @ 听说你家有一根很长的绳子，那绳子有多长呢？ It's said that you have a very long rope. How long is it?
☆Tee cheebbei seil seelkv ggv seiq. @ 今年她有三岁了。 She is three years old this year.

✧ me… ggv me niq 
◇短语, phr
●不能不…… cannot not (do sth), must (do sth):
☆Ngeq ggvzzeiq cheesiuq jjaiq pieq, xi gol yel me ruaq nal, ngaf lobia nee ddee shuq ceeq nee, me yel ggv me niq yil, teiq yel seiq. @ 我很喜欢这个东西，也舍不得给别人，但是我表哥来要又不能不给，所以就给他了。 I really like that thing and (I) was unwilling to give it to anyone else. But when my cousin came looking (for it), (I) had to give (it to him). So, (I) did.
●有，到，成(某种感觉、程度、样子等) to have, to attain (certain abstract qualities, characteristics or properties):
☆Feiji zzeeq chee seiq ggv shel, el zaq lei? @ 坐飞机的感觉怎么样，舒服吗？ How was flying in an airplane? Was it fun?
☆Baba dal me hof keel ye, jjuqdoq jjudo ggv ye. @ 看来这粑粑做得不好，硬邦邦的。 It seems as if this flatbread wasn't cooked right. It's as hard as can be.
☆Cheeni che ddaq qil chee Liljai lei jjuq nilniq ggv meil. @ 今天这么冷，感觉上好像是又回到丽江似的。 With today being so cold, it's like being back in Lijiang.

【leel】〔ɭɯ⁵⁵〕
◇助, ptcl
●(主题标记——一般(但不一定)用于带条件的词义，通常用来强调句子成分，带有“甚至”的意思) topicalizer; commonly used when a conditional meaning is involved, but not necessarily; often marks a sentence constituent as the focal argument conveying the idea of "even…" •这个词不能位于句子的起始位置，一定要跟随其他句子成分。 This word cannot occur as the first word in a clause, but must follow another clause constituent:
☆Ngeq xi che ddeegvl ddoq me jji dal messaq, mi leel me jji wei. @ 我不但没见过这样的人，连听都没听说过。 I've not only never seen this sort of a person before, (I) haven't even heard (of them).
☆Che bbei jjiq dal leel pielnil bbee sseil, bbei me naiq. @ 要是还要这样糟蹋房子，就别租了。 If (you) are just going to continue damaging the house, then (you) mustn't continue (renting it).
■参见{chee1, nvl1, seil, yi#4}
✧ leel waf seil 
◇短语, phr
●如果是 if it is
✧ leel… seil 
◇助, ptcl
●如果…… if…

☆Hualleiq cheemei ddeekaf rheeq nee fvl ddeemei rheq mai ye. @ 那只猫一会儿就抓到了一只老鼠。 This cat caught a rat after a short time.

shuq maiq meq. @ 家里忙的时候，就只能利用早晚的时间找点牛草了。 If things are busy at home, there is only time in the morning and evening to look for grass for the cows.

【melsee】〔mɤ⁵⁵sɿ³³〕
◇助, ptcl
●（未完成体，可用在肯定动词后） imperfective aspect; can be used with positive verbs •在否定句中，这个词的第一音节通常可以省略，只保留声调，致使前一音节变成升调，但意思不变。 When the verb is negative, the first syllable of this word may be deleted, leaving the tone. This tone attaches to the preceding syllable, which causes that syllable's mid or low tone to become a rising tone. The original meaning is retained:
☆Bbei me zzaiq melsee. @ （= Bbei me zzaif see.）还没做得成。 It still isn't completed.
☆Tee nikvl hal dal ggv melsee. @ 她才两岁多。 She is still only two years old.
■参见{see#8}

【When he speaks as if (it) is real, I almost believe (him).
☆Ngafggeeq nee jai sei na dal ggv melsei, nge zzee ddeegvl nee shel mei… @ 我们刚说完，我的一个朋友说…… We had just finished talking when my friend said…

【naiq'vf】〔na²¹vv¹³〕
◇助动, auxv
●想要(做)，打算(做) to want to (do), plan to (do); lit. should-consider •有副词修饰时，副词要放在“naiq”和“vf”之间。 When this word is modified by an adverb (e.g. not, very, only, etc.), the adverb is inserted between the syllables:
☆Cheeni che ddaq qil chee, bbei ggee naiq'vf keel ye. @ 今天这么冷，可能要下雪。 It is so cold today that it might snow (i.e. it seems as if it wants to snow).
☆Ngeq chee nikvl loq nee jelye ddeemerq ggeedda yil, jjiq ddeejjiq haiq naiq'vf. @ 我想在这几年里攒点钱买套房子。

【I'm thinking (I) would like to put away some money for the next few years to buy a house.
☆Sso cheegvl neif gge mil cheegvl dalda naiq'vf ye. @ 这个男人和这个女人要结婚了。 This man and this woman would like to get married.
■参见{bbeqmi}

■相关词{o#1}
■同义词{coqnal}
●同辈中的姐妹 traditional term used to refer to the female children in a family:
☆Naqxi seil o neiq nal shel ddu meq yil, elnigvl yi nal dal waq meq yil, yagof ebbvq ggeessee gge sher gol cacaq bbee me niq seiq. @ 我们纳西讲究骨肉之别，咱们俩只是姐妹(肉)，就不要回去干涉娘家兄弟(骨)的事了。

【Naxi speak of the "bone" and the "flesh". The two of us are "flesh" (i.e. female), so don't go and interfere in the brothers' affairs.
☆Naqxi seil, yagoq xi chee o neiq nal bbei teiq bbiu meq yil, sher jju ddu jju seil, o cheehual juq zzeeqggue ner nal, cheehual juq seil ddee nono neiq seil tal seiq. @ 纳西族人的亲戚分宗族和母系亲戚两种，遇事必须和宗族人商量，但对母系亲族则告知即可。 Naxi clans are divided into the "bone" (males) and the "flesh" (females). When there is an important matter, the males must discuss it, the females are content to just be told what is decided.
■相关词{o#1}

【nee】〔ɳɯ³³〕
◇后置, postp
●(夺格词，离格词) ablative case marker (includes ergative, source, instrumental, locational, time, etc.)
●◇后置, postp
●(施事的助词，作格词) ergative marker; marks the agent in a transitive clause:
☆Nge nee Kehail gol doqdo ser. @ 我喜欢抱着科翰。

【I like to hold Mark (in my arms).
■相关词{gol#1}
◇后置, postp
●(标示比较句的主语) marks the ablative or subject in a comparative sentence:
☆Ersherq chee'liu nee elchee seelliu jerq sherq. @ 这根筷子比其他三根长。 This chopstick is longer than those three
chopsticks.
☆Meixal nee Kehail jerq nikvl ddeeq. @ 美笑比科翰大两岁。 Heidi is two years older than Mark.
■相关词{jerq#1}
◇后置, postp
●(标示比较句的夺格) ablative of comparison; used between a verb and auxiliary verb to indicate comparison or even superlative:
☆Tee qeq lal la ser, qeq cee la ser, jjiq rher la ser nal, qeq cee nee ser seiq. @ 她喜欢打篮球，也喜欢踢足球和游泳，但最喜欢的还是踢足球。 She likes to play basketball. (She) also likes to play soccer and to swim, but (she) likes playing soccer best.
◇后置, postp
●从 source marker (i.e. from a place or time); used when movement in a direction or time is expressed:
☆Ngaf goq nee rhee loq bbee chee, kee jji ddubbei seil, mvseeldee nee jji bel naqfvl gol ba la tv me tal. @ 从我们家到城里，要是步行的话，从早上走到天黑也到不了。 If (I) were going to walk to town from my house, (I) could walk from morning till night and still not get there.
☆Si'qi luf nee si'qi sai gol tv bbei jjiq nil el jju lei? @ 从星期六到星期三有没有空房间？ Do (you) have any empty rooms from Saturday till Wednesday?
◇后置, postp
●(工具的助词) instrumental marker; indicates the instrument or tool used in an action:
☆Ersherq nee hopeil ggaiq. @ 用筷子夹菜。 Use chopsticks to grip the vegetables.
◇后置, postp
●(方位的助词) locational adverbial marker; used when the action takes place in one place (i.e. without a directional verb):
☆Gai cheerheeq ngeq ngaf go taf goq nee jjaiq bbiq bbei ddeenihal xeq seiq. @ 前一阵我很舒服地在我哥家休息了一段时间。 The last time I was at my elder brother's house, (I) rested comfortably for several days.
☆Seellialdail loq nee geeq laq meil? @ 装在塑料袋里边称好吗？ How about if (I) weigh (it) in the plastic bag?
◇后置, postp
●(时间的助词) time adverbial marker
●◇连, conj
●(绝对夺格，独立夺格，夺格的独立成分) ablative absolute; indicating the event(s) of the second clause results from or follows after the event(s) of the first
clause:
☆"Eq, hualleiq!" Ngeq leel shel me sei melsei nee, ngaf mo neif nge zzee nigvl bbei cheekaq nee shel mei, "Me waq, hualleiqddvq me." “ @ 哦，是人家的猫”。我还没说完，我妈妈和我的两个朋友都说：“不是嘛，是野猫。” I had not even finished saying, "Hey, a housecat!" when my mother and two friends all suddenly said, "No, (it's) a leopard cat."
☆Cheebbei chee ddeemerq cer zeeggeeq nee, bbaq mil la ddeemerq chuq keel ye. @ 可能是因为天气比较热，今年的庄稼熟得早些。 Perhaps it's because this year has been warmer that the crops are ripening a little early.
☆Nge gu'liu gguq nee, yiyuail loq cher'ee ddeemerq shuq bbee ner ye. @ 我的头很疼，得去医院找点药才行。(I) need to go to the hospital for some medicine, because my head hurts.

✧ nvlmei bbei 
◇短语, phr
●安慰 to comfort and encourage:
☆Ngeq cheeni ggvzzeiq pielpie yil, ngaf bba gai ddeemaiq rer mei, nge gge nvlmei lei bbei yel ceeq ye. @ 我今天弄坏了东西，有点怕我爸，但是他反而过来安慰我。 Today I broke something and was afraid (of what) my father (might say), but (he) actually comforted me.
✧ nvlmei bbiq 
◇短语, phr
●安心，内心轻松愉快(for one's) heart to be at ease, relieved, (for one's) heart to be light and at peace
✧ nvlmei cer

●动心，高兴，感动(for interest or enthusiasm) to be aroused, to be happy, to be moved:
☆Ngeq cheeni rhee loq nee ggvzzeiq jjaiq pieq gge ddeesiuq gobvl yil, sseidde bbei nvlmei cer seiqmei, haiq bbeqmi ye nal, jelye me bul. @ 我今天在城里看见挺喜欢的一样东西，很心动地想买，却没有带钱。 I was in town today when (I) saw something (I) really liked. (I) was excited about it and wanted to buy it, but (I) hadn't taken any money.
✧ nvlmei chee'loq me jjuq 
◇短语, phr
●心不在焉 inattentive or preoccupied:
☆Ngeq cheeni hopeil herl neiq mei nvlmei chee'loq me jjuq bbei ddeesher seeddv yil, laq herl seiq. @ 今天我切菜的时候，心不在焉的想别的事情，结果切了手。 I was cutting vegetables today and (my) mind was preoccupied with another matter, so (I) cut (my) hand.
✧ nvlmei coco

☆Cheeni rhee loq chezee tailtai neiq ddoq yil, nvlmei coco jjaiq chuq. @ 今天在城里发生一起车祸，我看见了，害怕得心跳都加快了。

【Today in town (I) saw a car
accident, and oh, did (my) heart race.

【o】〔ʔø³³〕
◇名, n
●骨，骨干 bone, shaft of a long bone •古旧意义。 Archaic meaning.
■同义词{so'lo}
●父系宗族 paternal clan (traditional term used to refer to one's father's relatives):
☆Naqxi chee ebba gge ebbvq ggeessee cheehu gol seil o bbei liuq, emei juq gge yagoq xi gol seil nal bbei liuq. Coq'o shel la che bbei ceeq mei seiq. @ 纳西人把父系宗族看成是骨，把母系亲属看成是肉，“家族”(父系)这个词就是这么来的。 Naxi consider the father's side of the family to be the "bone". The mother's side is considered the "flesh". This is where the term "paternal clan" comes from.
■相关词{nal#3}
■同义词{coq'o}
●同辈中的兄弟 traditional term used to refer to the male children of one generation in a family:
☆Naqxi o bbiu ddu. O bbiu chee ebbvq ggeessee xiddeeq bie pil seil, ddeejjef goq me zzeeq bbei mail bbiubbiu yil, wuha wuzzee, wujjiq wubbei shel neiq mei seiq. @ 纳西人兴分家，分家就是兄弟成家以后就分开，各过各的日子。 Naxi have the custom of "dividing the bone" (i.e. dividing households). "Dividing the bone" means that when brothers get married (they) no longer live together. (After they) split, each of them takes care of (their own) household affairs.
■相关词{nal#3}
✧ o bbiu 
◇短语, phr
●分家 to divide a household (when the sons marry)

【see】〔sɿ³³〕
◇副, adv
●•通常本词前一个中调或低调的音节要发升调。 This word is fairly unique in that it causes the mid or low tone of the preceding syllable to become a rising tone.
●先 first, earlier, before:
☆Haf see zzee laq, zzee pil, tei'ee lei liuq tal seiq. @ 先吃饭吧，吃完再看书。 First eat. Then, (you) can read a book.
●才 until, just:
☆Cheekaf see bbei sei mv lail? @ 现在才干完呀？ Did you finish just now?
☆Nimei ggvf see ddai lei ddiul, jjiq bvf see zzeifko lei ddv. @ 太阳落了才去追狐狸，口渴了才去挖井。

【seil】〔se⁵⁵〕
◇助, ptcl
●就(主题助词) then (developmental topicalizer; sequential - including logical; marking advancement when between clauses, and points of departure when following a sentence constituent) •通常本词前一个中调或低调的音节要发升调。 This word is fairly unique in that it triggers the mid or low tone of the preceding syllable to become a rising tone:
☆Bba'laq cher bbee seil, laqyelko ggvna bbei ggeq teiq diel tal maf. Che bbei ddee sheelshee dal neiq yi, meeq lei rhuq lee zoq. @ 要洗衣服就把袖子好好卷起来嘛！这样随便捋一捋，不一会就会掉下来的。 If you're going to wash clothes, (you) should roll (your) sleeves up well. If (you) only shove (them) up, (they) will slide back down.
☆Ngef seil lafzer nee zzee ser seiq; yeqmeil biq yeqmeil yiq. @ 我最喜欢吃辣椒了，越辣越好。 I like to eat hot peppers – the hotter the better.
■参见{chee1, heil, leel5, nvl1, teil, yi#4}

✧ seiq tal mei 
◇短语, phr

☆Ngvl cheenihal ddeemerq jigaiq zoq nal, seiq tal mei ddeezail baba yel. @ 这段时间您可能比较忙，但还是麻烦您尽量帮忙一下。 You are probably quite busy these days, but (you) could help (me) as much as (you're) able.
✧ Seiq waf lei? = Seiq waq ye lei? 
◇短语, phr
●怎么样？ How is/are…?
◇代, pron
●哪 which (e.g. person, place, thing, etc.)
■同义词{sseif}
✧ seiq ddeesiuq

●哪一种 what kind or sort:
☆Kel seiq ddeesiuq jju lei? @ 有哪一种篮子？ What kind of baskets do (you) have?
seiq】〔se²¹〕
◇助, ptcl
●了(用以表达与现时相关的行为状态的语气词) modal particle indicating a currently relevant state •有学者以为这个助词是完成体，但是大部分纳西动词基本上都有已完成的意思，而这个词却没有已完成的意思。 Some scholars have mistakenly considered this to be a perfective aspect particle, but the default aspect for many Naxi verbs is perfective. This particle does not carry a telic sense:
☆Bber zzeeq xi ceeq ye yil, zzeizzeiq balba gai gulgu yel tal seiq. @ 客人到了，请把桌

【子摆上吧。 The guests are arriving, so (you) may set the food on.
☆Cei jjiq nee zherl mil pil gge algv seil algvzherl waq seiq. @ 用盐水腌透的鸭蛋就是咸鸭蛋。 Duck eggs that have been pickled in salt water are salted duck eggs.
☆Chee gguq seil, nigvl bbei ello cheegvl gge geezheeq komi yil, nigvl bbei ssei zaq bbei xiyuq seiq. @ 从那以后，两人都听从这位老爷爷的话，过上了很幸福的生活。 After this, the two of them followed the old man's advice together and lived ever so happily.
seiq】〔se²¹〕

【wul】〔wu⁵⁵〕
◇副, adv
●回 return (used before direction verbs to indicate one is returning home) •在句子中，这个词通常可以省略成一个升调加到前一个音节，整个句子的意思不变。 In a sentence, this word may be partially deleted, becoming a floating tone that attaches to the preceding syllable. If the preceding syllable has a mid or low tone, it will be articulated as a rising tone. The original meaning is retained:
☆Tee taf nai gol ddee bbeq neiq pil seil, ebbamei gguq nee lei wul heq. @ 他亲了奶奶一下，就跟着爸爸妈妈回去了。 After he kissed his grandma, (he) went home with (his) parents.
